#	 ( ( all Romans  ) ( like ( all Italians ) ) ) 	 ( ( all Italians  ) ( fear ( all Germans ) ) ) 
#	 ( ( all Romans  ) ( like ( all Italians ) ) ) 	 ( ( all Italians  ) ( fear ( all children ) ) ) 
|	 ( ( all Romans  ) ( like ( all Europeans ) ) ) 	 ( ( all Italians  ) ( fear ( all Romans ) ) ) 
|	 ( ( all Romans  ) ( like ( all Europeans ) ) ) 	 ( ( all Italians  ) ( fear ( all Italians ) ) ) 
#	 ( ( all Romans  ) ( like ( all Europeans ) ) ) 	 ( ( all Italians  ) ( fear ( all Europeans ) ) ) 
#	 ( ( all Romans  ) ( like ( all Europeans ) ) ) 	 ( ( all Italians  ) ( fear ( all Germans ) ) ) 
#	 ( ( all Romans  ) ( like ( all Europeans ) ) ) 	 ( ( all Italians  ) ( fear ( all children ) ) ) 
#	 ( ( all Romans  ) ( like ( all Germans ) ) ) 	 ( ( all Italians  ) ( fear ( all Romans ) ) ) 
#	 ( ( all Romans  ) ( like ( all Germans ) ) ) 	 ( ( all Italians  ) ( fear ( all Italians ) ) )
